create table DG_Schema(
schema_ID int,
schema_name varchar(80),
description varchar(80),
create_date date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Schema_schema_ID_PK primary key (schema_ID));

insert into DG_Schema values(	1,'Zeota','Zeota','17-AUG-2021','08-OCT-2021');
insert into DG_Schema values(	2,'SP','SP','17-AUG-2021','08-OCT-2021');
insert into DG_Schema values(	3,'Prop','Prop','17-AUG-2021','08-OCT-2021');

create table DG_Tables(
Table_ID varchar(80),
Table_Name varchar(80),

modify_date date,
constraint DG_Tables_Table_ID_PK primary key (Table_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Tables_Database_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Database_ID) REFERENCES DG_Schema(schema_ID));

create table DG_Attributes(
Table_id varchar(80),
Table_Name varchar(80),
Attributes_ID varchar(80),
Attributes_Name	varchar(80),
comment	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Attributes_Attributes_ID_PK primary key (Attributes_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Attributes_Table_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Table_ID) REFERENCES DG_Tables(Table_ID));

create table DG_Attributes_ConstCheck(
Constraint_name varchar(80),
Constraint_Type varchar(80),
CC_ID	varchar(80),
Attributes_ID varchar(80),
Comment	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Attributes_ConstCheck_CC_ID_Attributes_ID_PK primary key (CC_ID,Attributes_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Attributes_ConstCheck_Attributes_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Attributes_ID) REFERENCES DG_Attributes(Attributes_ID));

create table DG_User_Unit_Role(	
User_ID varchar(80),
Role_ID varchar(80),
Unit_ID varchar(80),
definition	varchar(80),
start_date varchar(80),
end_date varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_User_Unit_Role_User_ID_Role_ID_Unit_ID_start_date_PK primary key (User_ID,Role_ID,Unit_ID,start_date),
CONSTRAINT DG_User_Unit_Role_User_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (User_ID) REFERENCES DG_Users(User_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_User_Unit_Role_Role_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Role_ID) REFERENCES DG_Role(Role_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_User_Unit_Role_Unit_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Unit_ID) REFERENCES DG_Unit(Unit_ID));

create table DG_Unit_Role_Table(
URT_ID varchar(80),
Table_id varchar(80),
Role_ID	varchar(80),
Unit_ID varchar(80),
DB_Operation varchar(80),
definition varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Unit_Role_Table_URT_ID_Table_id_Role_ID_Unit_ID_PK primary key (URT_ID,Table_id,Role_ID,Unit_ID,DB_Operation),
CONSTRAINT DG_Unit_Role_Table_Table_id_FK FOREIGN KEY (Table_id) REFERENCES DG_Tables(Table_id),
CONSTRAINT DG_Unit_Role_Table_Role_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Role_ID) REFERENCES DG_Role(Role_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Unit_Role_Table_Unit_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Unit_ID) REFERENCES DG_Unit(Unit_ID));

create table DG_Views(	
V_name varchar(80),
View_ID varchar(80),
description	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_View_Table_ID_View_ID_PK primary key (View_ID));


create table DG_View_Table(	
Table_ID varchar(80),
View_ID varchar(80),
description	varchar(80),
definition	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_View_Table_Table_ID_View_ID_PK primary key (Table_ID,View_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_View_Table_Table_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Table_ID) REFERENCES DG_Tables(Table_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_View_Table_View_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (View_ID) REFERENCES DG_Views(View_ID));

CONSTRAINT DG_Base_Trigger_Table_Table_ID_PK FOREIGN KEY (Table_ID) REFERENCES DG_Tables(Table_ID));

create table DG_DBMS(
DBMS_ID	varchar(80),
DBMS_Name varchar(80),
description varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_DBMS_DBMS_ID_PK primary key (DBMS_ID));

create table DG_DBMS_Version(
DBMS_V_ID varchar(80) unique,
DBMS_ID	varchar(80),
DBMS_Name varchar(80),
description varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_DBMS_ID_DBMS_V_ID_PK primary key (DBMS_V_ID, DBMS_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Tables_DBMS_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (DBMS_ID) REFERENCES DG_DBMS (DBMS_ID));

Create table DG_DBMS_Tables(
DBMS_V_ID	varchar(80),
DBMS_ID	varchar(80),
Table_id varchar(80),
Database_ID int,
description varchar(80),
comment varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
CONSTRAINT DG_DBMS_Tables_DBMS_ID_DBMS_V_ID_Table_ID_Database_ID_PK primary key (DBMS_V_ID, DBMS_ID,Database_ID,Table_id),
CONSTRAINT DG_DBMS_Tables_Table_id_FK FOREIGN KEY (Table_id) REFERENCES DG_Tables(Table_id),
CONSTRAINT DG_DBMS_Tables_DBMS_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (DBMS_ID) REFERENCES DG_DBMS(DBMS_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_DBMS_Tables_DBMS_V_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (DBMS_V_ID) REFERENCES DG_DBMS_Version(DBMS_V_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_DBMS_Tables_Database_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Database_ID) REFERENCES DG_Schema(schema_ID));


create table DG_DBMS_Table(
DBMS_ID	varchar(80),
Audit_ID varchar(80),
Table_id varchar(80),  
Database_ID int,
description varchar(80),
type_description varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
CONSTRAINT DG_DBMS_Table_DBMS_ID_Audit_T_ID_Table_ID_Database_ID_PK primary key (DBMS_ID,Audit_ID,Database_ID,Table_id ),
CONSTRAINT DG_DBMS_Table_Table_id_FK FOREIGN KEY (Table_id) REFERENCES DG_Tables(Table_id),
CONSTRAINT DG_DBMS_Table_DBMS_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (DBMS_ID) REFERENCES DG_DBMS(DBMS_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_DBMS_Table_Audit_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Audit_ID) REFERENCES DG_Audit_Table(Audit_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_DBMS_Table_Database_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Database_ID) REFERENCES DG_Schema(schema_ID));
